name:b‚Äçu‚Äçr‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçt‚Äçt
info:Deluxe Double Twin Room
info:Stayed in December 2023
info:Business travelers
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted December 13, 2023
msg:To find this hotel, exit the East gate of Shenzhen North rail station.   The hotel is just a short walk, maybe 100 yards at most, keeping to the left until you see a set of steps leading to an none descript entrance door of this super tall building.  The entrance does not say Pullman, but there is a large sign in Chinese that does say Pullman before the steps.     Once inside, there are signs posted in English directing you to  the elevators which take you to the lobby on the 46 floor.  Breakfast is ok, a bit of western (waffle/pancake/eggs, sausage,/ cerial), but mostly traditional chinese fair.   View is spectacular.    Room service easy with Q scan, portions are small and price is high.   Service attentive and English no issue.

In addition, next door to the hotel is the Bingo Space Shopping Mall (also on the lower floor of Shenzhen North Railway Station). It is not very big, but it has a variety of food, shopping and entertainment. We always had dinner here after visiting the zoo.

One stop away from Metro Line 5 is Hongshan Station, where there is Hongshan 6979 Shopping Mall.
It takes only 10 minutes to take a taxi to Longhua Yifangtiandi, which is very convenient.
Good value for money, will stay again in the future
